611→\tsubpath := route.Param(ctx, \"subpath\")\n   612→\n   613→\tif subpath == \"/pprof\" {\n   614→\t\thttp.Redirect(w, req, req.URL.Path+\"/\", http.StatusMovedPermanently)\n   615→\t\treturn\n   616→\t}\n   617→\n   618→\tif !strings.HasPrefix(subpath, \"/pprof/\") {\n   619→\t\thttp.NotFound(w, req)\n   620→\t\treturn\n   621→\t}\n   622→\tsubpath = strings.TrimPrefix(subpath, \"/pprof/\")\n   623→\n   624→\tswitch subpath {\n   625→\tcase \"cmdline\":\n   626→\t\tpprof.Cmdline(w, req)\n   627→\tcase \"profile\":\n   628→\t\tpprof.Profile(w, req)\n   629→\tcase \"symbol\":\n   630→\t\tpprof.Symbol(w, req)\n   631→\tcase \"trace\":\n   632→\t\tpprof.Trace(w, req)\n   633→\tcase \"fgprof\":\n   634→\t\tfgprofHandler.ServeHTTP(w, req)\n   635→\tdefault:\n   636→\t\treq.URL.Path = \"/debug/pprof/\" + subpath\n   637→\t\tpprof.Index(w, req)\n   638→\t}\n   639→}\n   640→\n   641→// SetReady sets the ready status of our web Handler.\n   642→func (h *Handler) SetReady(v ReadyStatus) {\n   643→\tif v == Ready {\n   644→\t\th.ready.Store(uint32(Ready))\n   645→\t\th.metrics.readyStatus.Set(1)\n   646→\t\treturn\n   647→\t}\n   648→\n   649→\th.ready.Store(uint32(v))\n   650→\th.metrics.readyStatus.Set(0)\n   651→}\n   652→\n   653→// Verifies whether the server is ready or not.\n   654→func (h *Handler) isReady() bool {\n   655→\treturn ReadyStatus(h.ready.Load()) == Ready\n   656→}\n   657→\n   658→// Checks if server is ready, calls f if it is, returns 503 if it is not.\n   659→func (h *Handler) testReady(f The function\n// will re-raise the error which will then be handled by the net/http package.\n// It is needed because the go-kit log package doesn't manage properly the\n// panics from net/http (see https://github.com/go-kit/kit/issues/233).\nfunc withStackTracer(h http.Handler, l *slog.Logger) http.Handler {\n\treturn http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tdefer *Handler) testReady(f http.HandlerFunc) http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tswitch ReadyStatus(h.ready.Load()) {\n\t\tcase Ready:\n\t\t\tf(w, r)\n\t\tcase Unavailable\")\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(w, \"Unknown state\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// Quit returns the receive-only quit channel.\nfunc (h listeners, err\n\t\t}\n\t\tlisteners = append(listeners, listener)\n\t}\n\treturn listeners, nil\n}\n\n// Listener creates the TCP listener for web requests.\nfunc (h *Handler) Listener(address (api_v1.RuntimeInfo, error) {\n\tstatus := api_v1.RuntimeInfo{\n\t\tStartTime:      h.birth,\n\t\tCWD:            h.cwd,\n\t\tGoroutineCount: runtime.NumGoroutine(),\n\t\tGOMAXPROCS:
